There seems to be a misunderstanding. The segment provided is not a single English sentence to be translated into Japanese. Instead, it appears to be a mix of English and Japanese, with a question at the end.  To clarify, the correct translation of "Resumption of the session" into Japanese is indeed "セッションの再開".  As for the question "Which language do all people in Europe speak?", the answer is that there is no single language spoken by all people in Europe. Europe is a multilingual continent with many languages spoken across different countries and regions. Some of the most widely spoken languages in Europe include English, Spanish, French, German, Italian, and Portuguese, among others.
